###########################
# USA Events By herkles
###########################

add_namespace = ustates

### Lead up to the Civil War ###
country_event = { # Black Monday hits America
	id = ustates.2
	title = ustates.2.t
	desc = ustates.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_run_on_the_banks

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usleadup.80 days = 69 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.2 option ustates.2.a"
		name = ustates.2.a
		add_stability = -0.1

		USA_increase_great_depression = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			HON = {
				country_event = { id = honduras.100 days = 10 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Father Charles Coughlin (PAP)
	id = ustates.17
	title = ustates.17.t
	desc = ustates.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_father_coughlin

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ask the President of the United States to shut down this 'Radio Priest'
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.17 option ustates.17.a"
		name = ustates.17.a
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_stability = -0.04
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = KR_pleased
		}
		USA = { country_event = ustates.18 }
	}
	option = { #It would be best if we did not interfere
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.17 option ustates.17.b"
		name = ustates.17.b
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_stability = 0.02
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Father Charles Coughlin's CBS Radio Broadcasts (USA)
	id = ustates.18
	title = ustates.18.t
	desc = ustates.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_father_coughlin

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.18 option ustates.18.a"
		name = ustates.18.a
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_political_power = -80
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_pleased
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.18 option ustates.18.b"
		name = ustates.18.b
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
	}
}

### Post-Civil War stuff ###
country_event = { # Victory for MacArthur
	id = ustates.116
	title = ustates.116.t
	desc = ustates.116.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_macarthur_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # macarthur keeps power
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.116 option ustates.116.a"
		name = ustates.116.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				country_exists = ACC
				ACC = { NOT = { owns_state = 373 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				country_exists = ACC
				ACC = { owns_state = 373 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CAESAR } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = macarthur_keeps_power_flag
		complete_national_focus = USA_american_caesar
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.05 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.134 days = 20 random_days = 40 }
			news_event = ustates.1017
		}
	}
	option = { # MacArthur gives up power
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.116 option ustates.116.b"
		name = ustates.116.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				country_exists = ACC
				ACC = { NOT = { owns_state = 373 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				country_exists = ACC
				ACC = { owns_state = 373 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CAESAR }
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = USA_ACW_macarthur }
			set_cosmetic_tag = USA_ACW_colourless
		}
		complete_national_focus = USA_democracy_triumphs
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.3
		}
		country_event = { id = ustates.136 days = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			ACC = { country_event = { id = ustates.121 days = 10 random_days = 20 } }
			news_event = ustates.1017
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Reconciliation with the USA
	id = ustates.121
	title = ustates.121.t
	desc = ustates.121.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_fireside_chats

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_elected_government = yes
		is_subject = no
		has_war = no
		USA = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			is_subject = no
		}
	}

	option = { # Join with America(Game Over)
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.121 option ustates.121.a"
		name = ustates.121.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				USA = {
					has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.6
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_WAR }
					has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_PEACE_PRISON }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				set_country_flag = ACC_peacefully_rejoined #country flag for ACC peacefully rejoining after MacArthur steps down
				country_event = { id = ustates.122 days = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				USA = {
					change_tag_from = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We are the true and legitimate America!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.121 option ustates.121.b"
		name = ustates.121.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_PEACE }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				country_event = { id = ustates.123 days = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The ACC has decided to rejoin America
	id = ustates.122
	title = ustates.122.t
	desc = ustates.122.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ACC_golden_gate_crowd

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject = no
		has_elected_government = yes
		ACC = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_elected_government = yes
			NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
		}
	}

	option = { # America is reunited!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.122 option ustates.122.a"
		name = ustates.122.a
		ACC = {
			transfer_navy = { target = USA }
			every_unit_leader = {
				demote_to_general = yes
				set_nationality = USA
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = ACC
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.1
	}
}

		}
	}

		text = ustates.127.d.elected
		trigger = {
			has_right_democratic_government = yes
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = macarthur_keeps_power_flag

		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6

			ideology = social_democrat

		}

			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_political_power = 20

			country_event = { id = ustates.128 days = 150 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The great Migration
	id = ustates.134
	title = ustates.134.t
	desc = ustates.134.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Continental_Map

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = macarthur_keeps_power_flag
		OR = {
			country_exists = ACC
			country_exists = NEE
			CAN = {
				has_democratic_government = yes
				any_owned_state = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = ACC }
			ACC = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { country_exists = NEE }
			NEE = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
		else = {
			CAN = {
				save_event_target_as = migrate
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # kill them
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.134 option ustates.134.a"
		name = ustates.134.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_great_migration1
			days = 90
		}
		add_manpower = -5000
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_stability = 0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:migrate = {
				country_event = { id = ustates.135 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Let them go
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.134 option ustates.134.b"
		name = ustates.134.b
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_war_support = -0.02
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_great_migration2
			days = 50
		}
		add_manpower = -2500
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:migrate = {
				country_event = { id = ustates.135 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Refugees from MacArthur(ACC)
	id = ustates.135
	title = ustates.135.t

	desc = {
		text = ustates.135.d.let_go
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_idea = USA_great_migration1
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.135.d.army
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_idea = USA_great_migration2
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_reconstruction

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Flavor
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.135 option ustates.135.a"
		name = ustates.135.a
		if = { # Big Mac let them go
			limit = {
				USA = { has_idea = USA_great_migration1 }
			}
			add_war_support = 0.05
			add_manpower = 3000
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = USA_great_migration3
				days = 90
			}
		}
		else = { # Big Mac killed them
			add_war_support = 0.15
			add_political_power = 50
			add_manpower = 5000
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = USA_great_migration4
				days = 50
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Provisional President
	id = ustates.136
	title = ustates.136.t
	desc = ustates.136.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Inauguration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { USA_election_year = 1936 }
		if = {
			limit = { date > 1948.11.8 }
			add_to_variable = { USA_election_year = 12 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { date > 1944.11.8 }
			add_to_variable = { USA_election_year = 8 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { date > 1940.11.8 }
			add_to_variable = { USA_election_year = 4 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Vandenberg
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.136 option ustates.136.a"
		name = ustates.136.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_olson_was_president
					has_country_flag = USA_long_was_president
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_MARLIB } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_SOCLIB } }
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?USA_election_year].11.08"
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = USA_arthur_vandenberg
			ideology = market_liberal_subtype
		}
		add_trait = {
			character = USA_arthur_vandenberg
			ideology = market_liberal_subtype
			trait = USA_shadow_president
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			USA_united_states_congress = {
				remove_trait = {
					trait = KR_authoritarian_sic
					slot = second_in_command
				}
				add_trait = {
					trait = KR_parliament_sic
					slot = second_in_command
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable = USA_election_year
	}

	option = { #Garner
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.136 option ustates.136.b"
		name = ustates.136.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_borah_was_president
					has_country_flag = USA_landon_was_president
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_SOCCON } }
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?USA_election_year].11.08"
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = USA_john_nance_garner
			ideology = social_conservative_subtype
		}
		add_trait = {
			character = USA_john_nance_garner
			ideology = social_conservative_subtype
			trait = USA_shadow_president
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			USA_united_states_congress = {
				remove_trait = {
					trait = KR_authoritarian_sic
					slot = second_in_command
				}
				add_trait = {
					trait = KR_parliament_sic
					slot = second_in_command
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable = USA_election_year
	}
}

country_event = { # Alaska Statehood
	id = ustates.153
	title = ustates.153.t
	desc = ustates.153.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_ccc_troop

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_puerto_rico_statehood }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # they are a state

		}

	desc = { # civil war happened, ACC formed(ACC)
		text = ustates.160.d.civil_war_acc_acc
		trigger = {
			tag = ACC
		}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = USA

country_event = { # William Borah Passes Away
	id = ustates.186
	title = ustates.186.t

	desc = {
		text = ustates.186.d.president.war
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = USA_william_borah }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.186.d.president.peace
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = USA_william_borah }
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.186.d.couped
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_borah_was_president
			has_country_flag = USA_macarthur_coup
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.186.d.nominee.coup
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_Borah_Nominated
			has_country_flag = USA_macarthur_coup
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_borah_was_president }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.186.d.nominee.nocoup
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_Borah_Nominated
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_borah_was_president }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_macarthur_coup }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.186.d.senator
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Borah_Nominated }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_William_Borah

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.186 option ustates.186.a"
		name = ustates.186.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_william_borah }
				has_character = USA_quentin_roosevelt
			}
			promote_character = USA_quentin_roosevelt
		}
		retire_character = USA_william_borah
		hidden_effect = {
			WCA = { country_event = ustates.185 }
			APG = { country_event = ustates.185 }
		}
	}
}

### 1940 Elections ###
country_event = {
	id = ustates.200 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_democratic_government = yes
		check_variable = { USA_election = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = USA_shadow_president
			}
			country_event = ustates.201 #MacArthur vs Byrd
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_quentin_roosevelt }
			}
			country_event = ustates.202 #Roosevelt vs Hoover/Long
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_alf_landon }
			}
			country_event = ustates.203 #Willkie vs Landon
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_arthur_vandenberg }
			}
			country_event = ustates.2030 #Vandenberg vs Hoover
		}
		else = {
			country_event = ustates.204 #Roosevelt vs Garner
		}
		add_to_variable = { USA_election = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { #MacArthur vs Byrd
	id = ustates.201
	title = ustates.201.t
	desc = ustates.201.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_MacArthur_Byrd

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Republican - MacArthur
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.201 option ustates.201.a"
		name = ustates.201.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_MARLIB } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = USA_shadow_president }
				remove_country_leader_trait = USA_shadow_president
			}
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = USA_douglas_macarthur
			ideology = market_liberal_subtype
		}
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = USA_harry_byrd
		}
	}

	option = { # Democrat - Byrd
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.201 option ustates.201.b"
		name = ustates.201.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_SOCCON } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_SOCLIB } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = USA_shadow_president }
				remove_country_leader_trait = USA_shadow_president
			}
		}
		promote_character = USA_harry_byrd
		USA_conservative_democrats_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = {
				character = USA_douglas_macarthur
				ideology = market_liberal_subtype
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Roosevelt vs Hoover/Long
	id = ustates.202
	title = {
		text = ustates.202.t.default
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character = APG_huey_long } }
	}
	title = {
		text = ustates.202.t.huey
		trigger = { has_character = APG_huey_long }
	}

	desc = {
		text = ustates.202.d.restored
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character = USA_douglas_macarthur } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.202.d.default
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character = APG_huey_long } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.202.d.huey
		trigger = { has_character = APG_huey_long }
	}

	picture = "[USA_Roosevelt_vs_Hoover_or_Long_event_picture]"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Republican - Roosevelt
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.202 option ustates.202.a"
		name = ustates.202.a
		promote_character = USA_quentin_roosevelt
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_MARLIB } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_SOCLIB } }
			}
		}
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = USA_herbert_hoover
			# Roosevelt's flavour events
			country_event = { id = ustates.175 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Democrat - Hoover
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.202 option ustates.202.b"
		name = ustates.202.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_character = APG_huey_long }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_SOCCON } }
			}
		}
		promote_character = USA_herbert_hoover
		USA_conservative_democrats_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = USA_quentin_roosevelt
			# Hoover's flavour events
			#country_event = { id = ustates.176 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
			#country_event = { id = ustates.177 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Democrat - Long
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.202 option ustates.202.c"
		name = ustates.202.c
		trigger = { has_character = APG_huey_long }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_path option = USA_PATH_AUTDEM } }
			}
		}
		APG_huey_long = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
		}
		USA_longist_democrats_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			APG_huey_long = {
				promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			# Hoover's flavour events
			#country_event = { id = ustates.176 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
			#country_event = { id = ustates.177 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
			APG_fire_long_events = yes
		}
		complete_national_focus = APG_every_man_a_king
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = APG_share_the_wealth_modifier }
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

### 1944 Elections ###
country_event = {
	id = ustates.205 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_democratic_government = yes
		check_variable = { USA_election = 2 }
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_herbert_hoover }
			}
			country_event = ustates.206 #Hoover vs Taft
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_john_nance_garner }
			}
			country_event = ustates.2060 #Garner vs Taft
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = APG_huey_long }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = APG_guide_american_democracy }
				country_event = ustates.223
			}
			else = {
				country_event = ustates.2061 #Long vs Taft
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_alben_barkley }
			}
			country_event = ustates.207 #Barkley vs Taft
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = USA_quentin_roosevelt }
					has_country_leader = { character = USA_alf_landon }
				}
			}
			country_event = ustates.208 #Lucas vs Roosevelt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_arthur_vandenberg }
			}
			country_event = ustates.2080 #Lucas vs Vandenberg
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_douglas_macarthur }
			}
			country_event = ustates.209 #MacArthur vs Russell Jr.
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_harry_byrd }
			}
			country_event = ustates.210 #Taft vs Byrd
		}
		else = {
			country_event = ustates.211 #Taft vs Russell Jr.
		}
		add_to_variable = { USA_election = 1 }
	}
}

### 1948 elections ###
country_event = {
	id = ustates.212 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_democratic_government = yes
		check_variable = { USA_election = 3 }
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_scott_lucas }
			}
			country_event = ustates.213 #Lucas vs Halleck
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_robert_taft }
			}
			country_event = ustates.214 #Taft vs Chandler
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_quentin_roosevelt }
			}
			country_event = ustates.215 #Roosevelt vs Chandler
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_richard_russell_jr }
			}
			country_event = ustates.216 #Halleck vs Russell Jr.
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = APG_huey_long }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = APG_guide_american_democracy }
				country_event = ustates.223
			}
			else = {
				country_event = ustates.2160 #Halleck vs Long
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = ustates.217 #Halleck vs Chandler
		}
		add_to_variable = { USA_election = 1 }
	}
}

### 1952 Elections ###
country_event = {
	id = ustates.218 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_democratic_government = yes
		check_variable = { USA_election = 4 }
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_charles_halleck }
			}
			country_event = ustates.219 #Douglas vs Halleck
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_happy_chandler }
			}
			country_event = ustates.220 #Stassen vs Chandler
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = APG_Huey_long }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = APG_guide_american_democracy }
				country_event = ustates.223
			}
			else = {
				country_event = ustates.2200 #Stassen vs Long
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = USA_richard_russell_jr }
			}
			country_event = ustates.221 #Stassen vs Sparkman
		}
		else = {
			country_event = ustates.222 #Douglas vs Stassen
		}
	}
}

### League of American States ###
country_event = { # Join the League?
	id = ustates.250
	title = ustates.250.t
	desc = ustates.250.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.250 option ustates.250.a"
		name = ustates.250.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						tag = CEN
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CEN_dem_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = COS
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = COS_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = CUB
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = CUB_FORPOL_WAIT } }
						OR = {
							AND = {
								FROM = { tag = USA }
								NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = CUB_FORPOL_USA } }
							}
							AND = {
								FROM = { tag = APG }
								NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = CUB_FORPOL_APG } }
							}
							AND = {
								FROM = { tag = ACC }
								NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = CUB_FORPOL_ACC } }
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						tag = DOM
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = DOM_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = HAI
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = HAI_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		effect_tooltip = { add_ideas = USA_league_of_america_1 }
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
			country_event = ustates.253
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.250 option ustates.250.b"
		name = ustates.250.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					AND = {
						tag = CEN
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CEN_dem_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = COS
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = COS_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = CUB
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = CUB_FORPOL_WAIT } }
						OR = {
							AND = {
								FROM = { tag = USA }
								NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = CUB_FORPOL_USA } }
							}
							AND = {
								FROM = { tag = APG }
								NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = CUB_FORPOL_APG } }
							}
							AND = {
								FROM = { tag = ACC }
								NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = CUB_forpol option = CUB_FORPOL_ACC } }
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						tag = DOM
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = DOM_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = HAI
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = HAI_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		FROM = { country_event = ustates.251 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Change League idea
	id = ustates.255
	title = ustates.255.t
	desc = ustates.255.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SWI_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_3 }
			check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 9 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_2 }
			OR = {
				check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 5 }
				check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 8 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_1 }
			OR = {
				check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 1 }
				check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 4 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 0 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.255 option ustates.255.a"
		name = ustates.255.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_3 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 1 } }
				remove_ideas = USA_league_head_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 5 } }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_3
					add_idea = USA_league_head_1
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_3
					add_idea = USA_league_head_2
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num < 1 } }
				remove_ideas = USA_league_head_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 8 } }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_2
					add_idea = USA_league_head_3
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_2
					add_idea = USA_league_head_1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = USA_league_head_1 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 8 } }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_1
					add_idea = USA_league_head_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 4 } }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = USA_league_head_1
					add_idea = USA_league_head_2
				}
			}
			else = {
				remove_ideas = USA_league_head_1
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 8 } }
				add_ideas = USA_league_head_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA.USA_loas_members^num > 4 } }
				add_ideas = USA_league_head_2
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = USA_league_head_1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # USA offers advisors
	id = ustates.260
	title = ustates.260.t
	desc = ustates.260.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_volunteers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FROM
			has_idea = USA_american_advisors_1
			has_idea = WCA_american_advisors_1
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_together_with = FROM
			any_enemy_country = { has_war_with = FROM }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.260 option ustates.260.a"
		name = ustates.260.a # Agree
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { original_tag = WCA } }
			add_ideas = WCA_american_advisors_1
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = USA_american_advisors_1
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { gives_military_access_to = FROM }
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
				}
				give_military_access = FROM
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { country_event = ustates.262 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.260 option ustates.260.b"
		name = ustates.260.b # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 100
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = ustates.261 }
	}
}

country_event = { # asking for New England Back
	id = ustates.270
	title = ustates.270.t
	desc = ustates.270.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_chicago

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_subject = NEE
			is_in_faction_with = NEE
			any_owned_state = { is_new_england = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { # Lets not risk a war.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.270 option ustates.270.a"
		name = ustates.270.a
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_subject = NEE }
				end_puppet = NEE
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
				NEE = { leave_faction = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = NEE }
				NEE = { separate_peace_all_wars = yes }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_new_england = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			FROM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = USA_agreed_nee_rejoin
			country_event = ustates.271
		}
	}
	option = { # We shall never give into yankee arrogance
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.270 option ustates.270.b"
		name = ustates.270.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = CAN_supports_@FROM
						is_ally_with = IMP
					}
					FROM = { has_country_flag = CAN_returned_land }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = CAN_joined_the_ACW
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
				any_enemy_country = {
					is_actual_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				country_exists = GBR
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_refused_new_england
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject = no
				}
				effect_tooltip = { leave_faction = yes }
			}
			country_event = ustates.272
		}
	}
}

		trigger = {

				original_tag = NFA
				original_tag = GER
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_mission

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Of course they may join!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.281 option ustates.281.a"

		add_political_power = 50
		add_to_faction = FROM
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = IMP }
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = USA_demanded_fee_payment }
			FROM = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_outraged }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
				remove_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = KR_trade_sanctions }
				FROM = {
					remove_opinion_modifier = { target = PREV modifier = KR_trade_sanctions }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We have no need of them
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.281 option ustates.281.b"
		name = ustates.281.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = ustates.282 days = 1 } }
	}
}

		392 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }

country_event = {
	id = ustates.513
	title = ustates.513.t
	desc = ustates.513.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.513 option ustates.513.a"
		name = ustates.513.a #Focus on Minnesota
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_minnesota_order }
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_minnesota_order
		382 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		391 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes

			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}

# USA proposed reunion
country_event = {
	id = ustates.530
	title = ustates.530.t
	desc = ustates.530.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_capitol_hill

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.530 option ustates.530.a"
		name = ustates.530.a #MacArthur did America a favor - we will rejoin, no questions asked
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = ACC_miss_ceasefire_name
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				USA = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_long_was_president } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_PEACE_PRISON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_WAR }
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.535 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.530 option ustates.530.b"
		name = ustates.530.b #Yes, let them know we demand MacArthur be imprisoned first
		trigger = {
			USA = { has_character = USA_douglas_macarthur }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = ACC_rocky_ceasefire_name
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_PEACE }
					has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_WAR }
				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.532 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.530 option ustates.530.c"
		name = ustates.530.c #We do not trust them, now or ever
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_WAR }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.531 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# ACC wants MacArthur Arrested First
country_event = {
	id = ustates.532
	title = ustates.532.t
	desc = ustates.532.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ACC_golden_gate_crowd

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = ACC }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.532 option ustates.532.a"
		name = ustates.532.a #For the good of America, let it be done
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = USA_douglas_macarthur } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ACC = { has_country_flag = ACC_miss_ceasefire_name }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				ACC = { has_country_flag = ACC_rocky_ceasefire_name }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_WAR }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = USA_shadow_president }
			remove_country_leader_trait = USA_shadow_president
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.10
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -0.1 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		country_event = { id = ustates.540 hours = 6 }
		ACC = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.534 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.532 option ustates.532.b"
		name = ustates.532.b #MacArthur is a hero - refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_long_was_president }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_macarthur_path option = USA_MACARTHUR_PATH_CINCINNATUS_PEACE_PRISON }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_considering_reunion
		add_political_power = 50
		ACC = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.533 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

		}

	}

		}
	}

		text = ustates.536.d.arrest
		trigger = {
			USA = { NOT = { has_character = USA_douglas_macarthur } }
		}
	}

	major = yes

		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.536.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Fourth of July
	id = ustates.538
	title = ustates.538.t
	desc = ustates.538.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_july_4th

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_fired_fourth_of_july }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = USA_fired_fourth_of_july days = 20 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ustates.538 days = 365 }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_american_tag = yes }
				country_event = ustates.538
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.538 option ustates.538.a"
		name = ustates.538.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
					NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag }
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 5
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -10
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# Trial of the US Generals/Admirals
	id = ustates.650
	title = ustates.650.t

	desc = {
		text = ustates.650.APG
		trigger = {
			tag = APG
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.650.ACC
		trigger = {
			tag = ACC
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_military_trial

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {# Pardon the Generals
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.650 option ustates.650.a"
		name = ustates.650.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ACC }
			USA = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = characters_will_be_recruited
				character_list_tooltip = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_character = USA_dwight_david_eisenhower
							is_character = USA_omar_nelson_bradley
							is_character = USA_clarence_ralph_huebner
							is_character = USA_lesley_james_mcnair
							is_character = USA_lloyd_ralston_fredendall
							is_character = USA_edwin_forrest_harding
							is_character = USA_john_clifford_hodges_lee
							is_character = USA_frank_jack_fletcher
							is_character = USA_thomas_cassin_kinkaid
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_character = USA_dwight_david_eisenhower
								is_character = USA_omar_nelson_bradley
								is_character = USA_clarence_ralph_huebner
								is_character = USA_lesley_james_mcnair
								is_character = USA_lloyd_ralston_fredendall
								is_character = USA_edwin_forrest_harding
								is_character = USA_john_clifford_hodges_lee
								is_character = USA_frank_jack_fletcher
								is_character = USA_thomas_cassin_kinkaid
							}
						}
						demote_to_general = yes
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = APG }
			USA = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = characters_will_be_recruited
				character_list_tooltip = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_character = USA_dwight_david_eisenhower
							is_character = USA_omar_nelson_bradley
							is_character = USA_clarence_ralph_huebner
							is_character = USA_joseph_warren_stilwell
							is_character = USA_leonard_townsend_gerow
							is_character = USA_walter_krueger
							is_character = USA_edwin_forrest_harding
							is_character = USA_frank_jack_fletcher
							is_character = USA_thomas_cassin_kinkaid
							ACC = { ACC_isaac_davis_white = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
							ACC = { ACC_albert_coady_wedemeyer = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
							ACC = { ACC_alexander_archer_vandegrift = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
							ACC = { ACC_george_windle_read_jr = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
							ACC = { ACC_ernest_joseph_king = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_character = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_character = USA_dwight_david_eisenhower
								is_character = USA_omar_nelson_bradley

								is_character = USA_edwin_forrest_harding

								is_character = USA_thomas_cassin_kinkaid
								ACC = { ACC_isaac_davis_white = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
								ACC = { ACC_albert_coady_wedemeyer = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
								ACC = { ACC_alexander_archer_vandegrift = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
								ACC = { ACC_george_windle_read_jr = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
								ACC = { ACC_ernest_joseph_king = { is_character = PREV.PREV } }
							}
						}
						demote_to_general = yes
						set_nationality = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -0.05 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
	}

	}

		ai_chance = { base = 0 }

			}
		}

	}

# American Civil War
news_event = {
	id = ustates.1000
	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ustates.1000" }
	title = ustates.1000.t
	picture = GFX_news_event_USA_second_american_civil_war

	desc = {
		text = ustates.1000.d.four_way
		trigger = {
			country_exists = APG
			country_exists = ACC
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.1000.d.three_way
		trigger = {
			country_exists = APG
			NOT = { country_exists = ACC }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ustates.1000.d.two_way
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = APG }
			NOT = { country_exists = ACC }
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_for_sender = no
	major = yes

	show_major = {
		is_american_tag = no
	}

	option = {
		name = ustates.1000.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 12
				name = american_civil_war_threat
			}
		}
	}
}

			USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_american_caesar }
		}
	}

		text = ustates.1017.d.dem

			USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_democracy_triumphs }

	}

		text = ustates.1017.d.junta

		}
	}

	option = { # Is this the end of American democracy?

			}
		}
	}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = USA_national_populist_party_union_long_tt
				name = USA_national_populist_party_union
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_union_long_tt
				name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_union
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = USA_national_populist_party_union_long
				name = USA_national_populist_party_union
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_union_long
				name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_union
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_variable = { USA.coalition_stability = 0.5 }
		USA_increase_political_crisis = yes
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event usleadup.50 option usleadup.50.a"
		name = usleadup.50.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_Olson_Nominated
				has_country_flag = USA_Landon_Nominated
				has_country_flag = USA_Talmadge_Nominated
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_Olson_Won_Popular_Vote
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_Thomas_Nominated
				has_country_flag = USA_Landon_Nominated
				has_country_flag = USA_Wheeler_Nominated
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_Long_Won_Popular_Vote
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = usleadup.51
		}
	}
}

	id = usleadup.59
	title = usleadup.59.t
	desc = {
		text = usleadup.59.d.olson
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_Olson_Nominated }
	}
	desc = {
		text = usleadup.59.d.thomas
		trigger = { has_country_flag = USA_Thomas_Nominated }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_floyd_olson = { unit_leader_event = { id = usleadup.67 days = 17 } }
			USA_william_borah = { unit_leader_event = { id = usleadup.68 days = 17 } }
			USA_alf_landon = { unit_leader_event = { id = usleadup.69 days = 17 } }
			APG_huey_long = { unit_leader_event = { id = usleadup.70 days = 17 } }
			country_event = { id = usleadup.71 days = 17 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Coalition with Farmer-Labor
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event usleadup.59 option usleadup.59.a"
		name = usleadup.59.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_ELECTION option = USA_ELECTION_OLSON } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_ELECTION option = DEFAULT } }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_Olson_Nominated
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usleadup.60 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = usleadup.65 days = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Olson_Won_Popular_Vote } }
				country_event = { id = usleadup.64 days = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Coalition with the Republicans
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event usleadup.59 option usleadup.59.b"
		name = usleadup.59.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_ELECTION option = USA_ELECTION_BORAH } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_ELECTION option = USA_ELECTION_LANDON } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_ELECTION option = DEFAULT } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_Borah_Nominated }
				country_event = { id = usleadup.61 days = 3 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = usleadup.62 days = 3 }
			}
			country_event = { id = usleadup.65 days = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_Olson_Won_Popular_Vote
						has_country_flag = USA_Long_Won_Popular_Vote
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = usleadup.64 days = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Coalition with Long
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event usleadup.59 option usleadup.59.c"
		name = usleadup.59.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_ELECTION option = USA_ELECTION_LONG } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = USA_ELECTION option = DEFAULT } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = usleadup.63 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = usleadup.65 days = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_Long_Won_Popular_Vote } }
				country_event = { id = usleadup.64 days = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # No coalition
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event usleadup.59 option usleadup.59.e"
		name = usleadup.59.e
		ai_chance = {

		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		ROOT = { has_country_flag = USA_olson_was_president }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.2 days = 4 }
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.299 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.210 days = 9 }
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.400 days = 10 }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			USA_al_smith = { retire = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event usleadup.67 option usleadup.67.a"
		name = usleadup.67.a
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			promote_character = {
				character = USA_floyd_olson
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SPA_gains_strength
		add_to_variable = { var = SPA_strength value = 1 }
		395 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
		394 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
		396 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
		393 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
		261 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
		929 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
		975 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
		360 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
		complete_national_focus = USA_president_olson
	}

country_event = { # Borah introduces Fair Deal Legislation
	id = uscrisis.51
	title = uscrisis.51.t
	desc = uscrisis.51.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_father_coxs_march_completed }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.52 days = 7 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.51 option uscrisis.51.a"
		name = uscrisis.51.a
		add_political_power = 10
	}
}

		add_stability = -0.10

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_iron_fist_flag }

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_lost_faith_in_administration_tooltip

			833 = { USA_increase_Long_state_support = yes }

			394 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
			396 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }
			393 = { USA_increase_SPA_state_support = yes }

#Re-Light The Western Torch

country_event = { # Approach to Negotiations
	id = uscrisis.57
	title = uscrisis.57.t
	desc = uscrisis.57.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_father_coxs_march_completed }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.58 days = 8 }
			set_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_long_defence = 5 }
			set_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_south_defence = 5 }
			set_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_soft_attack = 0 }
			set_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_hard_attack = 0 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.57 option uscrisis.57.a"
		name = uscrisis.57.a
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		set_country_flag = USA_borah_negotiations_soft
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_soft_x2_tooltip
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.57 option uscrisis.57.b"
		name = uscrisis.57.b
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		set_country_flag = USA_borah_negotiations_hard
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_hard_x2_tooltip
	}
}

country_event = { # Who to meet first
	id = uscrisis.58
	title = uscrisis.58.t
	desc = uscrisis.58.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference2

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_father_coxs_march_completed }
	}

	option = { # Long
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.58 option uscrisis.58.a"
		name = uscrisis.58.a
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.59 days = 6 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_negotiations_values_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_long_defence = USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_long_lose_defence_tooltip
	}
	option = { # The South
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.58 option uscrisis.58.b"
		name = uscrisis.58.b
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.62 days = 6 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_negotiations_values_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_south_defence = USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_south_lose_defence_tooltip
	}
}

country_event = { #  First Meeting with Long
	id = uscrisis.59
	title = uscrisis.59.t
	desc = uscrisis.59.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Long_Rally

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_father_coxs_march_completed }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.60 days = 4 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Promise Progressive Policies
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.59 option uscrisis.59.a"
		name = uscrisis.59.a
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_negotiations_values_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_borah_negotiations_soft
			}
			set_temp_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_soft_attack = USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_soft_attack = USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_gain_soft_attack_tooltip
	}
	option = { # Promise Patronage
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.59 option uscrisis.59.b"
		name = uscrisis.59.b
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_negotiations_values_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_borah_negotiations_hard
			}
			set_temp_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_hard_attack = USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { USA_borah_negotiations_hard_attack = USA_borah_negotiations_temp_var }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_gain_hard_attack_tooltip
	}
}

		}
		set_country_flag = USA_borah_negotiation_long_hard_south_soft
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_gain_hard_attack_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_borah_long_hard_south_soft_tooltip
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.110 option uscrisis.110.a"
		name = uscrisis.110.a

			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_CIVIL_WAR option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_THREE_SIDES }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				has_game_rule = { rule = USA_CIVIL_WAR option = USA_CIVIL_WAR_THREE_SIDES }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = uscrisis.114 days = 7 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_landon_focused_on_conservatives
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_landon_conservatives_result_tooltip
			random_list = {
				75 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_landon_success_tooltip
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = { id = uscrisis.114 days = 7 }
					}
				}
				25 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_landon_failure_tooltip
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = { id = uscrisis.105 days = 7 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_landon_success_tooltip
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = { id = uscrisis.114 days = 7 }
					}
				}
				50 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_landon_failure_tooltip
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = { id = uscrisis.105 days = 7 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Push on with F-L
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.110 option uscrisis.110.b"
		name = uscrisis.110.b
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_landon_middle_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.112 days = 7 }
		}

country_event = { # Union Party falls apart
	id = uscrisis.502
	title = uscrisis.502.t
	desc = uscrisis.502.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_APG_america_first

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { has_character = APG_huey_long }

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.504 days = 650 }
			country_event = { id = uscrisis.505 days = 415 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event uscrisis.502 option uscrisis.502.a"
		name = uscrisis.502.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_compromise_long_tt
				name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_compromise
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = USA_national_populist_party_compromise_long_tt
				name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_compromise
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_compromise_long
				name = USA_authoritarian_democrat_party_compromise
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = USA_national_populist_party_compromise_long
				name = USA_national_populist_party_compromise
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_borah_democrats_reunited
		APG_huey_long = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
		}
		remove_country_leader_role = {
			character = APG_huey_long
			ideology = national_populist_subtype
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
}
